Through time, painters have sold their art in order to buy time to make another painting, Otherwise wewouldn't have much art in the World today. Composers should have the same opportunety to make a living out of his or her music. Business men don't carry their goods or fortune out into the streets and say "Please help yourself". Noone will benefit from free acces to music, because good music is one the Things that make life worthliving, I think we all can agree on that. Free access will mean poor quality, because composers and will be forced to make music in their spare time.
